26   /** Info of a variable in a pattern: The named tree and its type */

29   /** Names of methods that are added unconditionally to case classes */
30   def isDesugaredCaseClassMethodName(name: Name)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
31     name == nme.copy || name.isSelectorName

35   class SetterParamTree extends DerivedTypeTree {
36     def derivedType(sym: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context) = sym.info.resultType
37   }
38 
39   class TypeRefTree extends DerivedTypeTree {
40     def derivedType(sym: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context) = sym.typeRef
41   }
42 
43   /** A type tree that computes its type from an existing parameter.
44    *  @param suffix  String difference between existing parameter (call it `P`) and parameter owning the
45    *                 DerivedTypeTree (call it `O`). We have: `O.name == P.name + suffix`.
46    */
47   class DerivedFromParamTree(suffix: String) extends DerivedTypeTree {
48 
49     /** Make sure that for all enclosing module classes their companion lasses
50      *  are completed. Reason: We need the constructor of such companion classes to
51      *  be completed so that OriginalSymbol attachments are pushed to DerivedTypeTrees
52      *  in apply/unapply methods.
53      */
54     override def ensureCompletions(implicit ctx: Context) =
55       if (!(ctx.owner is Package))
56         if (ctx.owner.isClass) {
57           ctx.owner.ensureCompleted()
58           if (ctx.owner is ModuleClass)
59             ctx.owner.linkedClass.ensureCompleted()
60         }
61         else ensureCompletions(ctx.outer)
62 
63     /** Return info of original symbol, where all references to siblings of the
64      *  original symbol (i.e. sibling and original symbol have the same owner)
65      *  are rewired to like-named* parameters or accessors in the scope enclosing
66      *  the current scope. The current scope is the scope owned by the defined symbol
67      *  itself, that's why we have to look one scope further out. If the resulting
68      *  type is an alias type, dealias it. This is necessary because the
69      *  accessor of a type parameter is a private type alias that cannot be accessed
70      *  from subclasses.
71      *
72      *  (*) like-named means:
73      *
74      *       parameter name  ==  reference name ++ suffix
75      */
76     def derivedType(sym: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
77       val relocate = new TypeMap {
78         val originalOwner = sym.owner
79         def apply(tp: Type) = tp match {
80           case tp: NamedType if tp.symbol.exists && (tp.symbol.owner eq originalOwner) =>
81             val defctx = ctx.outersIterator.dropWhile(_.scope eq ctx.scope).next()
82             var local = defctx.denotNamed(tp.name ++ suffix).suchThat(_.isParamOrAccessor).symbol
83             if (local.exists) (defctx.owner.thisType select local).dealias
84             else {
85               def msg =
86                 s"no matching symbol for ${tp.symbol.showLocated} in ${defctx.owner} / ${defctx.effectiveScope.toList}"
87               if (ctx.reporter.errorsReported) ErrorType(msg)
88               else throw new java.lang.Error(msg)
89             }
90           case _ =>
91             mapOver(tp)
92         }
93       }
94       relocate(sym.info)
95     }
96   }
97 
98   /** A type definition copied from `tdef` with a rhs typetree derived from it */
99   def derivedTypeParam(tdef: TypeDef, suffix: String = ""): TypeDef =
100     cpy.TypeDef(tdef)(
101       name = tdef.name ++ suffix,
102       rhs = new DerivedFromParamTree(suffix).withPos(tdef.rhs.pos).watching(tdef)
103     )
104 
105   /** A derived type definition watching `sym` */
106   def derivedTypeParam(sym: TypeSymbol)(implicit ctx: Context): TypeDef =
107     TypeDef(sym.name, new DerivedFromParamTree("").watching(sym)).withFlags(TypeParam)
108 
109   /** A value definition copied from `vdef` with a tpt typetree derived from it */
110   def derivedTermParam(vdef: ValDef) =
111     cpy.ValDef(vdef)(
112       tpt = new DerivedFromParamTree("") withPos vdef.tpt.pos watching vdef)

116   /**   var x: Int = expr
117    *  ==>
118    *    def x: Int = expr
119    *    def x_=($1: <TypeTree()>): Unit = ()
120    */
121   def valDef(vdef: ValDef)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
122     val ValDef(name, tpt, rhs) = vdef
123     val mods = vdef.mods
124     val setterNeeded =
125       (mods is Mutable) && ctx.owner.isClass && (!(mods is PrivateLocal) || (ctx.owner is Trait))
126     if (setterNeeded) {
127       // TODO: copy of vdef as getter needed?
128       // val getter = ValDef(mods, name, tpt, rhs) withPos vdef.pos?
129       // right now vdef maps via expandedTree to a thicket which concerns itself.
130       // I don't see a problem with that but if there is one we can avoid it by making a copy here.
131       val setterParam = makeSyntheticParameter(tpt = (new SetterParamTree).watching(vdef))
132       // The rhs gets filled in later, when field is generated and getter has parameters (see Memoize miniphase)
133       val setterRhs = if (vdef.rhs.isEmpty) EmptyTree else unitLiteral
134       val setter = cpy.DefDef(vdef)(
135         name     = name.setterName,
136         tparams  = Nil,
137         vparamss = (setterParam :: Nil) :: Nil,
138         tpt      = TypeTree(defn.UnitType),
139         rhs      = setterRhs
140       ).withMods((mods | Accessor) &~ CaseAccessor)
141       Thicket(vdef, setter)
142     }
143     else vdef
144   }
145 
146   def makeImplicitParameters(tpts: List[Tree], forPrimaryConstructor: Boolean = false)(implicit ctx: Context) =
147     for (tpt <- tpts) yield {
148        val paramFlags: FlagSet = if (forPrimaryConstructor) PrivateLocalParamAccessor else Param
149        val epname = EvidenceParamName.fresh()
150        ValDef(epname, tpt, EmptyTree).withFlags(paramFlags | Implicit)
151     }
152 
153   /** Expand context bounds to evidence params. E.g.,
154    *
155    *      def f[T >: L <: H : B](params)
156    *  ==>
157    *      def f[T >: L <: H](params)(implicit evidence$0: B[T])
158    *
159    *  Expand default arguments to default getters. E.g,
160    *
161    *      def f[T: B](x: Int = 1)(y: String = x + "m") = ...
162    *  ==>
163    *      def f[T](x: Int)(y: String)(implicit evidence$0: B[T]) = ...
164    *      def f$default$1[T] = 1
165    *      def f$default$2[T](x: Int) = x + "m"
166    */
167   private def defDef(meth: DefDef, isPrimaryConstructor: Boolean = false)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
168     val DefDef(name, tparams, vparamss, tpt, rhs) = meth
169     val mods = meth.mods
170     val epbuf = new ListBuffer[ValDef]
171     def desugarContextBounds(rhs: Tree): Tree = rhs match {
172       case ContextBounds(tbounds, cxbounds) =>
173         epbuf ++= makeImplicitParameters(cxbounds, isPrimaryConstructor)
174         tbounds
175       case LambdaTypeTree(tparams, body) =>
176         cpy.LambdaTypeTree(rhs)(tparams, desugarContextBounds(body))
177       case _ =>
178         rhs
179     }
180     val tparams1 = tparams mapConserve { tparam =>
181       cpy.TypeDef(tparam)(rhs = desugarContextBounds(tparam.rhs))
182     }
183 
184     val meth1 = addEvidenceParams(cpy.DefDef(meth)(tparams = tparams1), epbuf.toList)
185 
186     /** The longest prefix of parameter lists in vparamss whose total length does not exceed `n` */
187     def takeUpTo(vparamss: List[List[ValDef]], n: Int): List[List[ValDef]] = vparamss match {
188       case vparams :: vparamss1 =>
189         val len = vparams.length
190         if (n >= len) vparams :: takeUpTo(vparamss1, n - len) else Nil
191       case _ =>
192         Nil
193     }
194 
195     def normalizedVparamss = meth1.vparamss map (_ map (vparam =>
196       cpy.ValDef(vparam)(rhs = EmptyTree)))
197 
198     def dropContextBound(tparam: TypeDef) = tparam.rhs match {
199       case ContextBounds(tbounds, _) => cpy.TypeDef(tparam)(rhs = tbounds)
200       case _ => tparam
201     }
202 
203     def defaultGetters(vparamss: List[List[ValDef]], n: Int): List[DefDef] = vparamss match {
204       case (vparam :: vparams) :: vparamss1 =>
205         def defaultGetter: DefDef =
206           DefDef(
207             name = DefaultGetterName(meth.name, n),
208             tparams = meth.tparams.map(tparam => dropContextBound(toDefParam(tparam))),
209             vparamss = takeUpTo(normalizedVparamss.nestedMap(toDefParam), n),
210             tpt = TypeTree(),
211             rhs = vparam.rhs
212           )
213           .withMods(Modifiers(mods.flags & AccessFlags, mods.privateWithin))
214           .withFlags(Synthetic)
215         val rest = defaultGetters(vparams :: vparamss1, n + 1)
216         if (vparam.rhs.isEmpty) rest else defaultGetter :: rest
217       case Nil :: vparamss1 =>
218         defaultGetters(vparamss1, n)
219       case nil =>
220         Nil
221     }
222 
223     val defGetters = defaultGetters(vparamss, 0)
224     if (defGetters.isEmpty) meth1
225     else {
226       val meth2 = cpy.DefDef(meth1)(vparamss = normalizedVparamss)
227         .withMods(meth1.mods | DefaultParameterized)
228       Thicket(meth2 :: defGetters)
229     }
230   }
231 
232   // Add all evidence parameters in `params` as implicit parameters to `meth` */
233   private def addEvidenceParams(meth: DefDef, params: List[ValDef])(implicit ctx: Context): DefDef =
234     params match {
235       case Nil =>
236         meth
237       case evidenceParams =>
238         val vparamss1 = meth.vparamss.reverse match {
239           case (vparams @ (vparam :: _)) :: rvparamss if vparam.mods is Implicit =>
240             ((evidenceParams ++ vparams) :: rvparamss).reverse
241           case _ =>
242             meth.vparamss :+ evidenceParams
243         }
244         cpy.DefDef(meth)(vparamss = vparamss1)
245     }
246 
247   /** The implicit evidence parameters of `meth`, as generated by `desugar.defDef` */
248   private def evidenceParams(meth: DefDef)(implicit ctx: Context): List[ValDef] =
249     meth.vparamss.reverse match {
250       case (vparams @ (vparam :: _)) :: _ if vparam.mods is Implicit =>
251         vparams.dropWhile(!_.name.is(EvidenceParamName))
252       case _ =>
253         Nil
254     }
255 
256   @sharable private val synthetic = Modifiers(Synthetic)
257 
258   private def toDefParam(tparam: TypeDef): TypeDef =
259     tparam.withMods(tparam.rawMods & EmptyFlags | Param)
260   private def toDefParam(vparam: ValDef): ValDef =
261     vparam.withMods(vparam.rawMods & Implicit | Param)

263   /** The expansion of a class definition. See inline comments for what is involved */
264   def classDef(cdef: TypeDef)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
265     val className = checkNotReservedName(cdef).asTypeName
266     val impl @ Template(constr0, parents, self, _) = cdef.rhs
267     val mods = cdef.mods
268     val companionMods = mods
269         .withFlags((mods.flags & AccessFlags).toCommonFlags)
270         .withMods(Nil)
271 
272     var defaultGetters: List[Tree] = Nil
273 
274     def decompose(ddef: Tree): DefDef = ddef match {
275       case meth: DefDef => meth
276       case Thicket((meth: DefDef) :: defaults) =>
277         defaultGetters = defaults
278         meth
279     }
280 
281     val constr1 = decompose(defDef(constr0, isPrimaryConstructor = true))
282 
283     // The original type and value parameters in the constructor already have the flags
284     // needed to be type members (i.e. param, and possibly also private and local unless
285     // prefixed by type or val). `tparams` and `vparamss` are the type parameters that
286     // go in `constr`, the constructor after desugaring.
287 
288     /** Does `tree' look like a reference to AnyVal? Temporary test before we have inline classes */
289     def isAnyVal(tree: Tree): Boolean = tree match {
290       case Ident(tpnme.AnyVal) => true
291       case Select(qual, tpnme.AnyVal) => isScala(qual)
292       case _ => false
293     }
294     def isScala(tree: Tree): Boolean = tree match {
295       case Ident(nme.scala_) => true
296       case Select(Ident(nme.ROOTPKG), nme.scala_) => true
297       case _ => false
298     }
299 
300     val isCaseClass  = mods.is(Case) && !mods.is(Module)
301     val isCaseObject = mods.is(Case) && mods.is(Module)
302     val isImplicit = mods.is(Implicit)
303     val isEnum = mods.hasMod[Mod.Enum] && !mods.is(Module)
304     val isEnumCase = isLegalEnumCase(cdef)
305     val isValueClass = parents.nonEmpty && isAnyVal(parents.head)
306     // This is not watertight, but `extends AnyVal` will be replaced by `inline` later.
307 
308 
309     val originalTparams = constr1.tparams
310     val originalVparamss = constr1.vparamss
311     val constrTparams = originalTparams.map(toDefParam)
312     val constrVparamss =
313       if (originalVparamss.isEmpty) { // ensure parameter list is non-empty
314         if (isCaseClass) ctx.error(CaseClassMissingParamList(cdef), cdef.namePos)
315         ListOfNil
316       }
317       else originalVparamss.nestedMap(toDefParam)
318     val constr = cpy.DefDef(constr1)(tparams = constrTparams, vparamss = constrVparamss)
319 
320     // Add constructor type parameters and evidence implicit parameters
321     // to auxiliary constructors
322     val normalizedBody = impl.body map {
323       case ddef: DefDef if ddef.name.isConstructorName =>
324         decompose(
325           defDef(
326             addEvidenceParams(
327               cpy.DefDef(ddef)(tparams = constrTparams),
328               evidenceParams(constr1).map(toDefParam))))
329       case stat =>
330         stat
331     }
332     def anyRef = ref(defn.AnyRefAlias.typeRef)
333 
334     val derivedTparams = constrTparams.map(derivedTypeParam(_))
335     val derivedVparamss = constrVparamss.nestedMap(derivedTermParam(_))
336     val arity = constrVparamss.head.length
337 
338     val classTycon: Tree = new TypeRefTree // watching is set at end of method
339 
340     def appliedTypeTree(tycon: Tree, args: List[Tree]) =
341       (if (args.isEmpty) tycon else AppliedTypeTree(tycon, args))
342         .withPos(cdef.pos.startPos)
343 
344     def appliedRef(tycon: Tree, tparams: List[TypeDef] = constrTparams) =
345       appliedTypeTree(tycon, tparams map refOfDef)
346 
347     // a reference to the class type bound by `cdef`, with type parameters coming from the constructor
348     val classTypeRef = appliedRef(classTycon)
349 
350     // a reference to `enumClass`, with type parameters coming from the case constructor
351     lazy val enumClassTypeRef = enumClass.primaryConstructor.info match {
352       case info: PolyType =>
353         if (constrTparams.isEmpty)
354           interpolatedEnumParent(cdef.pos.startPos)
355         else if ((constrTparams.corresponds(info.paramNames))((param, name) => param.name == name))
356           appliedRef(enumClassRef)
357         else {
358           ctx.error(i"explicit extends clause needed because type parameters of case and enum class differ"
359               , cdef.pos.startPos)
360           appliedTypeTree(enumClassRef, constrTparams map (_ => anyRef))
361         }
362       case _ =>
363         enumClassRef
364     }
365 
366     // new C[Ts](paramss)
367     lazy val creatorExpr = New(classTypeRef, constrVparamss nestedMap refOfDef)
368 
369     // Methods to add to a case class C[..](p1: T1, ..., pN: Tn)(moreParams)
370     //     def _1 = this.p1
371     //     ...
372     //     def _N = this.pN
373     //     def copy(p1: T1 = p1: @uncheckedVariance, ...,
374     //              pN: TN = pN: @uncheckedVariance)(moreParams) =
375     //       new C[...](p1, ..., pN)(moreParams)
376     //
377     // Note: copy default parameters need @uncheckedVariance; see
378     // neg/t1843-variances.scala for a test case. The test would give
379     // two errors without @uncheckedVariance, one of them spurious.
380     val caseClassMeths = {
381       def syntheticProperty(name: TermName, rhs: Tree) =
382         DefDef(name, Nil, Nil, TypeTree(), rhs).withMods(synthetic)
383       def productElemMeths = {
384         val caseParams = constrVparamss.head.toArray
385         for (i <- 0 until arity if nme.selectorName(i) `ne` caseParams(i).name)
386         yield syntheticProperty(nme.selectorName(i), Select(This(EmptyTypeIdent), caseParams(i).name))
387       }
388       def enumTagMeths = if (isEnumCase) enumTagMeth(CaseKind.Class)._1 :: Nil else Nil
389       def copyMeths = {
390         def isRepeated(tree: Tree): Boolean = tree match {
391           case PostfixOp(_, Ident(tpnme.raw.STAR)) => true
392           case ByNameTypeTree(tree1) => isRepeated(tree1)
393           case _ => false
394         }
395         val hasRepeatedParam = constrVparamss.exists(_.exists {
396           case ValDef(_, tpt, _) => isRepeated(tpt)
397           case _ => false
398         })
399         if (mods.is(Abstract) || hasRepeatedParam) Nil  // cannot have default arguments for repeated parameters, hence copy method is not issued
400         else {
401           def copyDefault(vparam: ValDef) =
402             makeAnnotated("scala.annotation.unchecked.uncheckedVariance", refOfDef(vparam))
403           val copyFirstParams = derivedVparamss.head.map(vparam =>
404             cpy.ValDef(vparam)(rhs = copyDefault(vparam)))
405           val copyRestParamss = derivedVparamss.tail.nestedMap(vparam =>
406             cpy.ValDef(vparam)(rhs = EmptyTree))
407           DefDef(nme.copy, derivedTparams, copyFirstParams :: copyRestParamss, TypeTree(), creatorExpr)
408             .withMods(synthetic) :: Nil
409         }
410       }
411 
412       if (isCaseClass)
413         copyMeths ::: enumTagMeths ::: productElemMeths.toList
414       else Nil
415     }
416 
417     // Case classes and case objects get Product parents
418     var parents1 = parents
419     if (isEnumCase && parents.isEmpty)
420       parents1 = enumClassTypeRef :: Nil
421     if (isCaseClass | isCaseObject)
422       parents1 = parents1 :+ scalaDot(str.Product.toTypeName)
423     if (isEnum)
424       parents1 = parents1 :+ ref(defn.EnumType)
425 
426     // The Eq instance for an Enum class. For an enum class
427     //
428     //    enum class C[T1, ..., Tn]
429     //
430     // we generate:
431     //
432     //    implicit def eqInstance[T1$1, ..., Tn$1, T1$2, ..., Tn$2](implicit
433     //      ev1: Eq[T1$1, T1$2], ..., evn: Eq[Tn$1, Tn$2]])
434     //      : Eq[C[T1$1, ..., Tn$1], C[T1$2, ..., Tn$2]] = Eq
435     def eqInstance = {
436       val leftParams = constrTparams.map(derivedTypeParam(_, "$1"))
437       val rightParams = constrTparams.map(derivedTypeParam(_, "$2"))
438       val subInstances = (leftParams, rightParams).zipped.map((param1, param2) =>
439         appliedRef(ref(defn.EqType), List(param1, param2)))
440       DefDef(
441           name = nme.eqInstance,
442           tparams = leftParams ++ rightParams,
443           vparamss = List(makeImplicitParameters(subInstances)),
444           tpt = appliedTypeTree(ref(defn.EqType),
445               appliedRef(classTycon, leftParams) :: appliedRef(classTycon, rightParams) :: Nil),
446           rhs = ref(defn.EqModule.termRef)).withFlags(Synthetic | Implicit)
447     }
448     def eqInstances = if (isEnum) eqInstance :: Nil else Nil
449 
450     // The thicket which is the desugared version of the companion object
451     //     synthetic object C extends parentTpt { defs }
452     def companionDefs(parentTpt: Tree, defs: List[Tree]) =
453       moduleDef(
454         ModuleDef(
455           className.toTermName, Template(emptyConstructor, parentTpt :: Nil, EmptyValDef, defs))
456             .withMods(companionMods | Synthetic))
457       .withPos(cdef.pos).toList
458 
459     val companionMeths = defaultGetters ::: eqInstances
460 
461     // The companion object definitions, if a companion is needed, Nil otherwise.
462     // companion definitions include:
463     // 1. If class is a case class case class C[Ts](p1: T1, ..., pN: TN)(moreParams):
464     //     def apply[Ts](p1: T1, ..., pN: TN)(moreParams) = new C[Ts](p1, ..., pN)(moreParams)  (unless C is abstract)
465     //     def unapply[Ts]($1: C[Ts]) = $1
466     // 2. The default getters of the constructor
467     // The parent of the companion object of a non-parameterized case class
468     //     (T11, ..., T1N) => ... => (TM1, ..., TMN) => C
469     // For all other classes, the parent is AnyRef.
470     val companions =
471       if (isCaseClass) {
472         // The return type of the `apply` method
473         val (applyResultTpt, widenDefs) =
474           if (!isEnumCase)
475             (TypeTree(), Nil)
476           else if (parents.isEmpty || enumClass.typeParams.isEmpty)
477             (enumClassTypeRef, Nil)
478           else {
479             val tparams = enumClass.typeParams.map(derivedTypeParam)
480             enumApplyResult(cdef, parents, tparams, appliedRef(enumClassRef, tparams))
481           }
482 
483         val parent =
484           if (constrTparams.nonEmpty ||
485               constrVparamss.length > 1 ||
486               mods.is(Abstract) ||
487               constr.mods.is(Private)) anyRef
488           else
489             // todo: also use anyRef if constructor has a dependent method type (or rule that out)!
490             (constrVparamss :\ (if (isEnumCase) applyResultTpt else classTypeRef)) (
491               (vparams, restpe) => Function(vparams map (_.tpt), restpe))
492         def widenedCreatorExpr =
493           (creatorExpr /: widenDefs)((rhs, meth) => Apply(Ident(meth.name), rhs :: Nil))
494         val applyMeths =
495           if (mods is Abstract) Nil
496           else
497             DefDef(nme.apply, derivedTparams, derivedVparamss, applyResultTpt, widenedCreatorExpr)
498               .withFlags(Synthetic | (constr1.mods.flags & DefaultParameterized)) :: widenDefs
499         val unapplyMeth = {
500           val unapplyParam = makeSyntheticParameter(tpt = classTypeRef)
501           val unapplyRHS = if (arity == 0) Literal(Constant(true)) else Ident(unapplyParam.name)
502           DefDef(nme.unapply, derivedTparams, (unapplyParam :: Nil) :: Nil, TypeTree(), unapplyRHS)
503             .withMods(synthetic)
504         }
505         companionDefs(parent, applyMeths ::: unapplyMeth :: companionMeths)
506       }
507       else if (companionMeths.nonEmpty)
508         companionDefs(anyRef, companionMeths)
509       else if (isValueClass) {
510         constr0.vparamss match {
511           case (_ :: Nil) :: _ => companionDefs(anyRef, Nil)
512           case _ => Nil // error will be emitted in typer
513         }
514       }
515       else Nil
516 
517     // For an implicit class C[Ts](p11: T11, ..., p1N: T1N) ... (pM1: TM1, .., pMN: TMN), the method
518     //     synthetic implicit C[Ts](p11: T11, ..., p1N: T1N) ... (pM1: TM1, ..., pMN: TMN): C[Ts] =
519     //       new C[Ts](p11, ..., p1N) ... (pM1, ..., pMN) =
520     val implicitWrappers =
521       if (!isImplicit)
522         Nil
523       else if (ctx.owner is Package) {
524         ctx.error(TopLevelImplicitClass(cdef), cdef.pos)
525         Nil
526       }
527       else if (isCaseClass) {
528         ctx.error(ImplicitCaseClass(cdef), cdef.pos)
529         Nil
530       }
531       else if (arity != 1) {
532         ctx.error(ImplicitClassPrimaryConstructorArity(), cdef.pos)
533         Nil
534       }
535       else
536         // implicit wrapper is typechecked in same scope as constructor, so
537         // we can reuse the constructor parameters; no derived params are needed.
538         DefDef(className.toTermName, constrTparams, constrVparamss, classTypeRef, creatorExpr)
539           .withMods(companionMods | Synthetic | Implicit)
540           .withPos(cdef.pos) :: Nil
541 
542     val self1 = {
543       val selfType = if (self.tpt.isEmpty) classTypeRef else self.tpt
544       if (self.isEmpty) self
545       else cpy.ValDef(self)(tpt = selfType).withMods(self.mods | SelfName)
546     }
547 
548     val cdef1 = addEnumFlags {
549       val originalTparamsIt = originalTparams.toIterator
550       val originalVparamsIt = originalVparamss.toIterator.flatten
551       val tparamAccessors = derivedTparams.map(_.withMods(originalTparamsIt.next().mods))
552       val caseAccessor = if (isCaseClass) CaseAccessor else EmptyFlags
553       val vparamAccessors = derivedVparamss match {
554         case first :: rest =>
555           first.map(_.withMods(originalVparamsIt.next().mods | caseAccessor)) ++
556           rest.flatten.map(_.withMods(originalVparamsIt.next().mods))
557         case _ =>
558           Nil
559       }
560       cpy.TypeDef(cdef)(
561         name = className,
562         rhs = cpy.Template(impl)(constr, parents1, self1,
563           tparamAccessors ::: vparamAccessors ::: normalizedBody ::: caseClassMeths))
564     }
565 
566     // install the watch on classTycon
567     classTycon match {
568       case tycon: DerivedTypeTree => tycon.watching(cdef1)
569       case _ =>
570     }
571 
572     flatTree(cdef1 :: companions ::: implicitWrappers)
573   }
574 
575   val AccessOrSynthetic = AccessFlags | Synthetic
576 
577   /** Expand
578    *
579    *    object name extends parents { self => body }
580    *
581    *  to:
582    *    <module> val name: name$ = New(name$)
583    *    <module> final class name$ extends parents { self: name.type => body }
584    */
585   def moduleDef(mdef: ModuleDef)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
586     val moduleName = checkNotReservedName(mdef).asTermName
587     val impl = mdef.impl
588     val mods = mdef.mods
589     lazy val isEnumCase = isLegalEnumCase(mdef)
590     if (mods is Package)
591       PackageDef(Ident(moduleName), cpy.ModuleDef(mdef)(nme.PACKAGE, impl).withMods(mods &~ Package) :: Nil)
592     else if (isEnumCase)
593       expandEnumModule(moduleName, impl, mods, mdef.pos)
594     else {
595       val clsName = moduleName.moduleClassName
596       val clsRef = Ident(clsName)
597       val modul = ValDef(moduleName, clsRef, New(clsRef, Nil))
598         .withMods(mods.toTermFlags & RetainedModuleValFlags | ModuleValCreationFlags)
599         .withPos(mdef.pos.startPos)
600       val ValDef(selfName, selfTpt, _) = impl.self
601       val selfMods = impl.self.mods
602       if (!selfTpt.isEmpty) ctx.error(ObjectMayNotHaveSelfType(mdef), impl.self.pos)
603       val clsSelf = ValDef(selfName, SingletonTypeTree(Ident(moduleName)), impl.self.rhs)
604         .withMods(selfMods)
605         .withPos(impl.self.pos orElse impl.pos.startPos)
606       val clsTmpl = cpy.Template(impl)(self = clsSelf, body = impl.body)
607       val cls = TypeDef(clsName, clsTmpl)
608         .withMods(mods.toTypeFlags & RetainedModuleClassFlags | ModuleClassCreationFlags)
609       Thicket(modul, classDef(cls).withPos(mdef.pos))
610     }
611   }
612 
613   /** The name of `mdef`, after checking that it does not redefine a Scala core class.
614    *  If it does redefine, issue an error and return a mangled name instead of the original one.
615    */
616   def checkNotReservedName(mdef: MemberDef)(implicit ctx: Context): Name = {
617     val name = mdef.name
618     if (ctx.owner == defn.ScalaPackageClass && defn.reservedScalaClassNames.contains(name.toTypeName)) {
619       def kind = if (name.isTypeName) "class" else "object"
620       ctx.error(em"illegal redefinition of standard $kind $name", mdef.pos)
621       name.errorName
622     }
623     else name
624   }
625 
626   /**     val p1, ..., pN: T = E
627    *  ==>
628    *      makePatDef[[val p1: T1 = E]]; ...; makePatDef[[val pN: TN = E]]
629    *
630    *      case e1, ..., eN
631    *  ==>
632    *      expandSimpleEnumCase([case e1]); ...; expandSimpleEnumCase([case eN])
633    */
634   def patDef(pdef: PatDef)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = flatTree {
635     val PatDef(mods, pats, tpt, rhs) = pdef
636     if (mods.hasMod[Mod.EnumCase] && enumCaseIsLegal(pdef))
637       pats map {
638         case id: Ident =>
639           expandSimpleEnumCase(id.name.asTermName, mods,
640             Position(pdef.pos.start, id.pos.end, id.pos.start))
641     }
642     else {
643       val pats1 = if (tpt.isEmpty) pats else pats map (Typed(_, tpt))
644       pats1 map (makePatDef(pdef, mods, _, rhs))
645     }
646   }
647 
648   /** If `pat` is a variable pattern,
649    *
650    *    val/var/lazy val p = e
651    *
652    *  Otherwise, in case there is exactly one variable x_1 in pattern
653    *   val/var/lazy val p = e  ==>  val/var/lazy val x_1 = (e: @unchecked) match (case p => (x_1))
654    *
655    *   in case there are zero or more than one variables in pattern
656    *   val/var/lazy p = e  ==>  private[this] synthetic [lazy] val t$ = (e: @unchecked) match (case p => (x_1, ..., x_N))
657    *                   val/var/def x_1 = t$._1
658    *                   ...
659    *                   val/var/def x_N = t$._N
660    *  If the original pattern variable carries a type annotation, so does the corresponding
661    *  ValDef or DefDef.
662    */
663   def makePatDef(original: Tree, mods: Modifiers, pat: Tree, rhs: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = pat match {
664     case IdPattern(named, tpt) =>
665       derivedValDef(original, named, tpt, rhs, mods)
666     case _ =>
667       val rhsUnchecked = makeAnnotated("scala.unchecked", rhs)
668       val vars = getVariables(pat)
669       val isMatchingTuple: Tree => Boolean = {
670         case Tuple(es) => es.length == vars.length
671         case _ => false
672       }
673       val ids = for ((named, _) <- vars) yield Ident(named.name)
674       val caseDef = CaseDef(pat, EmptyTree, makeTuple(ids))
675       val matchExpr =
676         if (forallResults(rhs, isMatchingTuple)) rhs
677         else Match(rhsUnchecked, caseDef :: Nil)
678       vars match {
679         case Nil =>
680           matchExpr
681         case (named, tpt) :: Nil =>
682           derivedValDef(original, named, tpt, matchExpr, mods)
683         case _ =>
684           val tmpName = UniqueName.fresh()
685           val patMods =
686             mods & Lazy | Synthetic | (if (ctx.owner.isClass) PrivateLocal else EmptyFlags)
687           val firstDef =
688             ValDef(tmpName, TypeTree(), matchExpr)
689               .withPos(pat.pos.union(rhs.pos)).withMods(patMods)
690           def selector(n: Int) = Select(Ident(tmpName), nme.selectorName(n))
691           val restDefs =
692             for (((named, tpt), n) <- vars.zipWithIndex)
693             yield
694               if (mods is Lazy) derivedDefDef(original, named, tpt, selector(n), mods &~ Lazy)
695               else derivedValDef(original, named, tpt, selector(n), mods)
696           flatTree(firstDef :: restDefs)
697       }
698   }
699 
700   /** Expand variable identifier x to x @ _ */
701   def patternVar(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
702     val Ident(name) = tree
703     Bind(name, Ident(nme.WILDCARD)).withPos(tree.pos)
704   }
705 
706   def defTree(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = tree match {
707     case tree: ValDef => valDef(tree)
708     case tree: TypeDef => if (tree.isClassDef) classDef(tree) else tree
709     case tree: DefDef =>
710       if (tree.name.isConstructorName) tree // was already handled by enclosing classDef
711       else defDef(tree)
712     case tree: ModuleDef => moduleDef(tree)
713     case tree: PatDef => patDef(tree)
714   }
715 
716   /**     { stats; <empty > }
717    *  ==>
718    *      { stats; () }
719    */
720   def block(tree: Block)(implicit ctx: Context): Block = tree.expr match {
721     case EmptyTree =>
722       cpy.Block(tree)(tree.stats,
723         unitLiteral withPos (if (tree.stats.isEmpty) tree.pos else tree.pos.endPos))
724     case _ =>
725       tree
726   }
727 
728   /** Translate infix operation expression
729     *
730     *     l op r     ==>    l.op(r)  if op is left-associative
731     *                ==>    r.op(l)  if op is right-associative
732     */
733   def binop(left: Tree, op: Ident, right: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Apply = {
734     def assignToNamedArg(arg: Tree) = arg match {
735       case Assign(Ident(name), rhs) => cpy.NamedArg(arg)(name, rhs)
736       case _ => arg
737     }
738     def makeOp(fn: Tree, arg: Tree, selectPos: Position) = {
739       val args: List[Tree] = arg match {
740         case Parens(arg) => assignToNamedArg(arg) :: Nil
741         case Tuple(args) => args.mapConserve(assignToNamedArg)
742         case _ => arg :: Nil
743       }
744       Apply(Select(fn, op.name).withPos(selectPos), args)
745     }
746 
747     if (isLeftAssoc(op.name))
748       makeOp(left, right, Position(left.pos.start, op.pos.end, op.pos.start))
749     else
750       makeOp(right, left, Position(op.pos.start, right.pos.end))
751   }
752 
753   /** Make closure corresponding to function.
754    *      params => body
755    *  ==>
756    *      def $anonfun(params) = body
757    *      Closure($anonfun)
758    *
759    *  If `inlineable` is true, tag $anonfun with an @inline annotation.
760    */
761   def makeClosure(params: List[ValDef], body: Tree, tpt: Tree = TypeTree(), inlineable: Boolean)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
762     var mods = synthetic
763     if (inlineable) mods |= Inline
764     Block(
765       DefDef(nme.ANON_FUN, Nil, params :: Nil, tpt, body).withMods(mods),
766       Closure(Nil, Ident(nme.ANON_FUN), EmptyTree))
767   }
768 
769   /** If `nparams` == 1, expand partial function
770    *
771    *       { cases }
772    *  ==>
773    *       x$1 => (x$1 @unchecked) match { cases }
774    *
775    *  If `nparams` != 1, expand instead to
776    *
777    *       (x$1, ..., x$n) => (x$0, ..., x${n-1} @unchecked) match { cases }
778    */
779   def makeCaseLambda(cases: List[CaseDef], nparams: Int = 1, unchecked: Boolean = true)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
780     val params = (1 to nparams).toList.map(makeSyntheticParameter(_))
781     val selector = makeTuple(params.map(p => Ident(p.name)))
782 
783     if (unchecked)
784       Function(params, Match(Annotated(selector, New(ref(defn.UncheckedAnnotType))), cases))
785     else
786       Function(params, Match(selector, cases))
787   }
788 
789   /** Map n-ary function `(p1, ..., pn) => body` where n != 1 to unary function as follows:
790    *
791    *    x$1 => {
792    *      def p1 = x$1._1
793    *      ...
794    *      def pn = x$1._n
795    *      body
796    *    }
797    */
798   def makeTupledFunction(params: List[ValDef], body: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
799     val param = makeSyntheticParameter()
800     def selector(n: Int) = Select(refOfDef(param), nme.selectorName(n))
801     val vdefs =
802       params.zipWithIndex.map{
803         case (param, idx) =>
804           DefDef(param.name, Nil, Nil, TypeTree(), selector(idx)).withPos(param.pos)
805       }
806     Function(param :: Nil, Block(vdefs, body))
807   }
808 
809   def makeImplicitFunction(formals: List[Type], body: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
810     val params = makeImplicitParameters(formals.map(TypeTree))
811     new ImplicitFunction(params, body)
812   }
813 
814   /** Add annotation to tree:
815    *      tree @fullName
816    *
817    *  The annotation is usually represented as a TypeTree referring to the class
818    *  with the given name `fullName`. However, if the annotation matches a file name
819    *  that is still to be entered, the annotation is represented as a cascade of `Selects`
820    *  following `fullName`. This is necessary so that we avoid reading an annotation from
821    *  the classpath that is also compiled from source.
822    */
823   def makeAnnotated(fullName: String, tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
824     val parts = fullName.split('.')
825     val ttree = ctx.typerPhase match {
826       case phase: FrontEnd if phase.stillToBeEntered(parts.last) =>
827         val prefix =
828           ((Ident(nme.ROOTPKG): Tree) /: parts.init)((qual, name) =>
829             Select(qual, name.toTermName))
830         Select(prefix, parts.last.toTypeName)
831       case _ =>
832         TypeTree(ctx.requiredClass(fullName).typeRef)
833     }
834     Annotated(tree, untpd.New(ttree, Nil))
835   }
836 
837   private def derivedValDef(original: Tree, named: NameTree, tpt: Tree, rhs: Tree, mods: Modifiers)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
838     val vdef = ValDef(named.name.asTermName, tpt, rhs)
839       .withMods(mods)
840       .withPos(original.pos.withPoint(named.pos.start))
841     val mayNeedSetter = valDef(vdef)
842     mayNeedSetter
843    }
844 
845   private def derivedDefDef(original: Tree, named: NameTree, tpt: Tree, rhs: Tree, mods: Modifiers) =
846     DefDef(named.name.asTermName, Nil, Nil, tpt, rhs)
847       .withMods(mods)
848       .withPos(original.pos.withPoint(named.pos.start))
849 
850   /** Main desugaring method */
851   def apply(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
852 
853     /**    { label def lname(): Unit = rhs; call }
854      */
855     def labelDefAndCall(lname: TermName, rhs: Tree, call: Tree) = {
856       val ldef = DefDef(lname, Nil, ListOfNil, TypeTree(defn.UnitType), rhs).withFlags(Label | Synthetic)
857       Block(ldef, call)
858     }
859 
860     /** Create tree for for-comprehension `<for (enums) do body>` or
861      *   `<for (enums) yield body>` where mapName and flatMapName are chosen
862      *  corresponding to whether this is a for-do or a for-yield.
863      *  The creation performs the following rewrite rules:
864      *
865      *  1.
866      *
867      *    for (P <- G) E   ==>   G.foreach (P => E)
868      *
869      *     Here and in the following (P => E) is interpreted as the function (P => E)
870      *     if P is a variable pattern and as the partial function { case P => E } otherwise.
871      *
872      *  2.
873      *
874      *    for (P <- G) yield E  ==>  G.map (P => E)
875      *
876      *  3.
877      *
878      *    for (P_1 <- G_1; P_2 <- G_2; ...) ...
879      *      ==>
880      *    G_1.flatMap (P_1 => for (P_2 <- G_2; ...) ...)
881      *
882      *  4.
883      *
884      *    for (P <- G; E; ...) ...
885      *      =>
886      *    for (P <- G.filter (P => E); ...) ...
887      *
888      *  5. For any N:
889      *
890      *    for (P_1 <- G; P_2 = E_2; val P_N = E_N; ...)
891      *      ==>
892      *    for (TupleN(P_1, P_2, ... P_N) <-
893      *      for (x_1 @ P_1 <- G) yield {
894      *        val x_2 @ P_2 = E_2
895      *        ...
896      *        val x_N & P_N = E_N
897      *        TupleN(x_1, ..., x_N)
898      *      } ...)
899      *
900      *    If any of the P_i are variable patterns, the corresponding `x_i @ P_i` is not generated
901      *    and the variable constituting P_i is used instead of x_i
902      *
903      *  @param mapName      The name to be used for maps (either map or foreach)
904      *  @param flatMapName  The name to be used for flatMaps (either flatMap or foreach)
905      *  @param enums        The enumerators in the for expression
906      *  @param body         The body of the for expression
907      */
908     def makeFor(mapName: TermName, flatMapName: TermName, enums: List[Tree], body: Tree): Tree = trace(i"make for ${ForYield(enums, body)}", show = true) {
909 
910       /** Make a function value pat => body.
911        *  If pat is a var pattern id: T then this gives (id: T) => body
912        *  Otherwise this gives { case pat => body }
913        */
914       def makeLambda(pat: Tree, body: Tree): Tree = pat match {
915         case IdPattern(named, tpt) =>
916           Function(derivedValDef(pat, named, tpt, EmptyTree, Modifiers(Param)) :: Nil, body)
917         case _ =>
918           makeCaseLambda(CaseDef(pat, EmptyTree, body) :: Nil)
919       }
920 
921       /** If `pat` is not an Identifier, a Typed(Ident, _), or a Bind, wrap
922        *  it in a Bind with a fresh name. Return the transformed pattern, and the identifier
923        *  that refers to the bound variable for the pattern.
924        */
925       def makeIdPat(pat: Tree): (Tree, Ident) = pat match {
926         case Bind(name, _) => (pat, Ident(name))
927         case id: Ident if isVarPattern(id) && id.name != nme.WILDCARD => (id, id)
928         case Typed(id: Ident, _) if isVarPattern(id) && id.name != nme.WILDCARD => (pat, id)
929         case _ =>
930           val name = UniqueName.fresh()
931           (Bind(name, pat), Ident(name))
932       }
933 
934       /** Add MaybeFilter attachment */
935       def orFilter(tree: Tree): tree.type = {
936         tree.putAttachment(MaybeFilter, ())
937         tree
938       }
939 
940       /** Make a pattern filter:
941        *    rhs.withFilter { case pat => true case _ => false }
942        *
943        *  On handling irrefutable patterns:
944        *  The idea is to wait until the pattern matcher sees a call
945        *
946        *      xs withFilter { cases }
947        *
948        *  where cases can be proven to be refutable i.e. cases would be
949        *  equivalent to  { case _ => true }
950        *
951        *  In that case, compile to
952        *
953        *      xs withFilter alwaysTrue
954        *
955        *  where `alwaysTrue` is a predefined function value:
956        *
957        *      val alwaysTrue: Any => Boolean = true
958        *
959        *  In the libraries operations can take advantage of alwaysTrue to shortcircuit the
960        *  withFilter call.
961        *
962        *  def withFilter(f: Elem => Boolean) =
963        *    if (f eq alwaysTrue) this // or rather identity filter monadic applied to this
964        *    else real withFilter
965        */
966       def makePatFilter(rhs: Tree, pat: Tree): Tree = {
967         val cases = List(
968           CaseDef(pat, EmptyTree, Literal(Constant(true))),
969           CaseDef(Ident(nme.WILDCARD), EmptyTree, Literal(Constant(false))))
970         Apply(orFilter(Select(rhs, nme.withFilter)), makeCaseLambda(cases))
971       }
972 
973       /** Is pattern `pat` irrefutable when matched against `rhs`?
974        *  We only can do a simple syntactic check here; a more refined check
975        *  is done later in the pattern matcher (see discussion in @makePatFilter).
976        */
977       def isIrrefutable(pat: Tree, rhs: Tree): Boolean = {
978         def matchesTuple(pats: List[Tree], rhs: Tree): Boolean = rhs match {
979           case Tuple(trees) => (pats corresponds trees)(isIrrefutable)
980           case Parens(rhs1) => matchesTuple(pats, rhs1)
981           case Block(_, rhs1) => matchesTuple(pats, rhs1)
982           case If(_, thenp, elsep) => matchesTuple(pats, thenp) && matchesTuple(pats, elsep)
983           case Match(_, cases) => cases forall (matchesTuple(pats, _))
984           case CaseDef(_, _, rhs1) => matchesTuple(pats, rhs1)
985           case Throw(_) => true
986           case _ => false
987         }
988         pat match {
989           case Bind(_, pat1) => isIrrefutable(pat1, rhs)
990           case Parens(pat1) => isIrrefutable(pat1, rhs)
991           case Tuple(pats) => matchesTuple(pats, rhs)
992           case _ => isVarPattern(pat)
993         }
994       }
995 
996       def isIrrefutableGenFrom(gen: GenFrom): Boolean =
997         gen.isInstanceOf[IrrefutableGenFrom] ||
998         IdPattern.unapply(gen.pat).isDefined ||
999         isIrrefutable(gen.pat, gen.expr)
1000 
1001       /** rhs.name with a pattern filter on rhs unless `pat` is irrefutable when
1002        *  matched against `rhs`.
1003        */
1004       def rhsSelect(gen: GenFrom, name: TermName) = {
1005         val rhs = if (isIrrefutableGenFrom(gen)) gen.expr else makePatFilter(gen.expr, gen.pat)
1006         Select(rhs, name)
1007       }
1008 
1009       enums match {
1010         case (gen: GenFrom) :: Nil =>
1011           Apply(rhsSelect(gen, mapName), makeLambda(gen.pat, body))
1012         case (gen: GenFrom) :: (rest @ (GenFrom(_, _) :: _)) =>
1013           val cont = makeFor(mapName, flatMapName, rest, body)
1014           Apply(rhsSelect(gen, flatMapName), makeLambda(gen.pat, cont))
1015         case (GenFrom(pat, rhs)) :: (rest @ GenAlias(_, _) :: _) =>
1016           val (valeqs, rest1) = rest.span(_.isInstanceOf[GenAlias])
1017           val pats = valeqs map { case GenAlias(pat, _) => pat }
1018           val rhss = valeqs map { case GenAlias(_, rhs) => rhs }
1019           val (defpat0, id0) = makeIdPat(pat)
1020           val (defpats, ids) = (pats map makeIdPat).unzip
1021           val pdefs = (valeqs, defpats, rhss).zipped.map(makePatDef(_, Modifiers(), _, _))
1022           val rhs1 = makeFor(nme.map, nme.flatMap, GenFrom(defpat0, rhs) :: Nil, Block(pdefs, makeTuple(id0 :: ids)))
1023           val allpats = pat :: pats
1024           val vfrom1 = new IrrefutableGenFrom(makeTuple(allpats), rhs1)
1025           makeFor(mapName, flatMapName, vfrom1 :: rest1, body)
1026         case (gen: GenFrom) :: test :: rest =>
1027           val filtered = Apply(orFilter(rhsSelect(gen, nme.withFilter)), makeLambda(gen.pat, test))
1028           val genFrom =
1029             if (isIrrefutableGenFrom(gen)) new IrrefutableGenFrom(gen.pat, filtered)
1030             else GenFrom(gen.pat, filtered)
1031           makeFor(mapName, flatMapName, genFrom :: rest, body)
1032         case _ =>
1033           EmptyTree //may happen for erroneous input
1034       }
1035     }
1036 
1037     // begin desugar
1038 
1039     // Special case for `Parens` desugaring: unlike all the desugarings below,
1040     // its output is not a new tree but an existing one whose position should
1041     // be preserved, so we shouldn't call `withPos` on it.
1042     tree match {
1043       case Parens(t) =>
1044         return t
1045       case _ =>
1046     }
1047 
1048     val desugared = tree match {
1049       case SymbolLit(str) =>
1050         Literal(Constant(scala.Symbol(str)))
1051       case InterpolatedString(id, segments) =>
1052         val strs = segments map {
1053           case ts: Thicket => ts.trees.head
1054           case t => t
1055         }
1056         val elems = segments flatMap {
1057           case ts: Thicket => ts.trees.tail
1058           case t => Nil
1059         } map {
1060           case Block(Nil, expr) => expr // important for interpolated string as patterns, see i1773.scala
1061           case t => t
1062         }
1063 
1064         Apply(Select(Apply(Ident(nme.StringContext), strs), id), elems)
1065       case InfixOp(l, op, r) =>
1066         if (ctx.mode is Mode.Type)
1067           if (!op.isBackquoted && op.name == tpnme.raw.AMP) AndTypeTree(l, r)     // l & r
1068           else if (!op.isBackquoted && op.name == tpnme.raw.BAR) OrTypeTree(l, r) // l | r
1069           else AppliedTypeTree(op, l :: r :: Nil) // op[l, r]
1070         else {
1071           assert(ctx.mode is Mode.Pattern) // expressions are handled separately by `binop`
1072           Apply(op, l :: r :: Nil) // op(l, r)
1073         }
1074       case PostfixOp(t, op) =>
1075         if ((ctx.mode is Mode.Type) && !op.isBackquoted && op.name == tpnme.raw.STAR) {
1076           val seqType = if (ctx.compilationUnit.isJava) defn.ArrayType else defn.SeqType
1077           Annotated(
1078             AppliedTypeTree(ref(seqType), t),
1079             New(ref(defn.RepeatedAnnotType), Nil :: Nil))
1080         } else {
1081           assert(ctx.mode.isExpr || ctx.reporter.hasErrors || ctx.mode.is(Mode.Interactive), ctx.mode)
1082           Select(t, op.name)
1083         }
1084       case PrefixOp(op, t) =>
1085         val nspace = if (ctx.mode.is(Mode.Type)) tpnme else nme
1086         Select(t, nspace.UNARY_PREFIX ++ op.name)
1087       case Tuple(ts) =>
1088         val arity = ts.length
1089         def tupleTypeRef = defn.TupleType(arity)
1090         if (arity > Definitions.MaxTupleArity) {
1091           ctx.error(TupleTooLong(ts), tree.pos)
1092           unitLiteral
1093         } else if (arity == 1) ts.head
1094         else if (ctx.mode is Mode.Type) AppliedTypeTree(ref(tupleTypeRef), ts)
1095         else if (arity == 0) unitLiteral
1096         else Apply(ref(tupleTypeRef.classSymbol.companionModule.termRef), ts)
1097       case WhileDo(cond, body) =>
1098         // { <label> def while$(): Unit = if (cond) { body; while$() } ; while$() }
1099         val call = Apply(Ident(nme.WHILE_PREFIX), Nil).withPos(tree.pos)
1100         val rhs = If(cond, Block(body, call), unitLiteral)
1101         labelDefAndCall(nme.WHILE_PREFIX, rhs, call)
1102       case DoWhile(body, cond) =>
1103         // { label def doWhile$(): Unit = { body; if (cond) doWhile$() } ; doWhile$() }
1104         val call = Apply(Ident(nme.DO_WHILE_PREFIX), Nil).withPos(tree.pos)
1105         val rhs = Block(body, If(cond, call, unitLiteral))
1106         labelDefAndCall(nme.DO_WHILE_PREFIX, rhs, call)
1107       case ForDo(enums, body) =>
1108         makeFor(nme.foreach, nme.foreach, enums, body) orElse tree
1109       case ForYield(enums, body) =>
1110         makeFor(nme.map, nme.flatMap, enums, body) orElse tree
1111       case PatDef(mods, pats, tpt, rhs) =>
1112         val pats1 = if (tpt.isEmpty) pats else pats map (Typed(_, tpt))
1113         flatTree(pats1 map (makePatDef(tree, mods, _, rhs)))
1114       case ParsedTry(body, handler, finalizer) =>
1115         handler match {
1116           case Match(EmptyTree, cases) => Try(body, cases, finalizer)
1117           case EmptyTree => Try(body, Nil, finalizer)
1118           case _ =>
1119             Try(body,
1120               List(CaseDef(Ident(nme.DEFAULT_EXCEPTION_NAME), EmptyTree, Apply(handler, Ident(nme.DEFAULT_EXCEPTION_NAME)))),
1121               finalizer)
1122         }
1123     }
1124     desugared.withPos(tree.pos)
1125   }
1126 
1127   /** Create a class definition with the same info as the refined type given by `parent`
1128    *  and `refinements`.
1129    *
1130    *      parent { refinements }
1131    *  ==>
1132    *      trait <refinement> extends core { this: self => refinements }
1133    *
1134    *  Here, `core` is the (possibly parameterized) class part of `parent`.
1135    *  If `parent` is the same as `core`, self is empty. Otherwise `self` is `parent`.
1136    *
1137    *  Example: Given
1138    *
1139    *      class C
1140    *      type T1 = C { type T <: A }
1141    *
1142    *  the refined type
1143    *
1144    *      T1 { type T <: B }
1145    *
1146    *  is expanded to
1147    *
1148    *      trait <refinement> extends C { this: T1 => type T <: A }
1149    *
1150    *  The result of this method is used for validity checking, is thrown away afterwards.
1151    *  @param parent  The type of `parent`
1152    */
1153   def refinedTypeToClass(parent: tpd.Tree, refinements: List[Tree])(implicit ctx: Context): TypeDef = {
1154     def stripToCore(tp: Type): List[Type] = tp match {
1155       case tp: AppliedType => tp :: Nil
1156       case tp: TypeRef if tp.symbol.isClass => tp :: Nil     // monomorphic class type
1157       case tp: TypeProxy => stripToCore(tp.underlying)
1158       case AndType(tp1, tp2) => stripToCore(tp1) ::: stripToCore(tp2)
1159       case _ => defn.AnyType :: Nil
1160     }
1161     val parentCores = stripToCore(parent.tpe)
1162     val untpdParent = TypedSplice(parent)
1163     val (classParents, self) =
1164       if (parentCores.length == 1 && (parent.tpe eq parentCores.head)) (untpdParent :: Nil, EmptyValDef)
1165       else (parentCores map TypeTree, ValDef(nme.WILDCARD, untpdParent, EmptyTree))
1166     val impl = Template(emptyConstructor, classParents, self, refinements)
1167     TypeDef(tpnme.REFINE_CLASS, impl).withFlags(Trait)
1168   }
1169 
1170  /** If tree is of the form `id` or `id: T`, return its name and type, otherwise return None.
1171    */
1172   private object IdPattern {
1173     def unapply(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Option[VarInfo] = tree match {
1174       case id: Ident => Some(id, TypeTree())
1175       case Typed(id: Ident, tpt) => Some((id, tpt))
1176       case _ => None
1177     }
1178   }
1179 
1180   /** Returns list of all pattern variables, possibly with their types,
1181    *  without duplicates
1182    */
1183   private def getVariables(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): List[VarInfo] = {
1184     val buf = new ListBuffer[VarInfo]
1185     def seenName(name: Name) = buf exists (_._1.name == name)
1186     def add(named: NameTree, t: Tree): Unit =
1187       if (!seenName(named.name)) buf += ((named, t))
1188     def collect(tree: Tree): Unit = tree match {
1189       case Bind(nme.WILDCARD, tree1) =>
1190         collect(tree1)
1191       case tree @ Bind(_, Typed(tree1, tpt)) if !mayBeTypePat(tpt) =>
1192         add(tree, tpt)
1193         collect(tree1)
1194       case tree @ Bind(_, tree1) =>
1195         add(tree, TypeTree())
1196         collect(tree1)
1197       case Typed(id: Ident, t) if isVarPattern(id) && id.name != nme.WILDCARD && !isWildcardStarArg(tree) =>
1198         add(id, t)
1199       case id: Ident if isVarPattern(id) && id.name != nme.WILDCARD =>
1200         add(id, TypeTree())
1201       case Apply(_, args) =>
1202         args foreach collect
1203       case Typed(expr, _) =>
1204         collect(expr)
1205       case NamedArg(_, arg) =>
1206         collect(arg)
1207       case SeqLiteral(elems, _) =>
1208         elems foreach collect
1209       case Alternative(trees) =>
1210         for (tree <- trees; (vble, _) <- getVariables(tree))
1211           ctx.error(IllegalVariableInPatternAlternative(), vble.pos)
1212       case Annotated(arg, _) =>
1213         collect(arg)
1214       case InterpolatedString(_, segments) =>
1215         segments foreach collect
1216       case InfixOp(left, _, right) =>
1217         collect(left)
1218         collect(right)
1219       case PrefixOp(_, od) =>
1220         collect(od)
1221       case Parens(tree) =>
1222         collect(tree)
1223       case Tuple(trees) =>
1224         trees foreach collect
1225       case Thicket(trees) =>
1226         trees foreach collect
1227       case Block(Nil, expr) =>
1228         collect(expr)
1229       case _ =>
1230     }
1231     collect(tree)
1232     buf.toList
1233   }
1234

1236 }
